    "an idempotented form @xmath0 of the quantum enveloping algebra of @xmath1 was introduced by beilinson - lusztig - macpherson  @xcite , who also related it to the geometry of partial flag varieties .",
    "this idempotented form was later extended by lusztig to the idempotented version @xmath2 of the quantum group @xmath3 associated to a kac - moody algebra @xmath4  @xcite .",
    "lusztig also constructed a basis in @xmath2 generalizing the canonical basis  @xcite in @xmath5 .",
    "multiplication and comultiplication in @xmath6 have positive integral coefficients in the lusztig canonical basis .",
    "these results led to the visionary conjecture of igor frenkel that @xmath2 could be categorified at generic @xmath7 in a purely algebraic and combinatorial fashion .",
    "frenkel s key insight was that the canonical basis should play a fundamental role , lifting to become a collection of simple objects of some category .",
    "one of the motivations for this conjecture was lusztig s realization  @xcite of the canonical basis for @xmath5 via simple perverse sheaves on lusztig quiver varieties .",
    "frenkel s proposal initiated the research program into categorification of quantum groups and their applications .",
    "crane and frenkel further conjectured the existence of a categorification of @xmath8 when @xmath7 was a root of unity ( this is still an open problem ) .",
    "part of their conjecture included potential applications of categorified quantum groups to the construction of 4-dimensional topological quantum field theories@xcite .",
    "a categorification of @xmath9 at generic @xmath7 was achieved by the second author in @xcite demonstrating that the quantum enveloping algebra of @xmath10 is just a shadow of a much richer algebraic structure .",
    "a @xmath11-linear 2-category @xmath12 was defined whose split grothendieck ring was shown to be isomorphic to the integral version of @xmath13 .",
    "the 2-category @xmath12 is the idempotent completion , or karoubi envelope , of a 2-category @xmath14 defined in terms of a graphical calculus .",
    "the objects @xmath15 of @xmath14 are parameterized by the weight lattice of @xmath16 . for @xmath17 with @xmath18",
    "the 1-morphisms from @xmath19 to @xmath20 are given by directs sums of 1-morphisms @xmath21 where @xmath22 , @xmath23 and @xmath24 .",
    "for @xmath11 a field , the 2-morphisms are given by @xmath11-linear combinations of certain planar diagrams modulo local relations .",
    "it was shown  @xcite that the isomorphism classes of indecomposable 1-morphisms ( up to grading shift ) in @xmath12 bijectively correspond to elements in lusztig s canonical basis .",
    "the 2-category @xmath12 was extended to a 2-category @xmath25 associated to an arbitrary root datum by the first two authors  @xcite generalizing their earlier work categorifying one - half of the quantum group associated to a symmetrizable kac - moody algebra  @xcite . for root datum associated to @xmath26",
    "it was shown that the 2-category @xmath12 categorifies the idempotented form of @xmath27 .    in this paper",
    "we extend the graphical calculus to the karoubi envelope to allow explicit decompositions of 1-morphisms into indecomposable 1-morphisms in @xmath12 ( theorems  [ thm_cal_eaeb ] and [ eq_cat_eafb ] ) . while the 2-category @xmath14 is naturally described in terms of a graphical calculus , there was previously no such purely diagrammatic description of its karoubi envelope @xmath12 . as a consequence of the explicit decompositions in this article ,",
    "we extend the main categorification result in @xcite to the case where @xmath28 , see corollary  [ cor_overz ] .",
    "we also obtain an explicit basis for the space of 2-morphisms between indecomposable 1-morphisms in section  [ sec_basis ] .",
    "the extended graphical calculus reveals further surprising connections between symmetric functions and the combinatorics encoded in the relations of the 2-category @xmath14 . in (",
    "* proposition 8.2 ) it was shown that there is an isomorphism @xmath29 ^ -{\\cong } & \\lambda,}\\ ] ] where @xmath30 is the graded ring of symmetric functions in countably many variables .",
    "a 2-morphism in @xmath31 is represented in the graphical calculus by a closed diagram .",
    "any such diagram can be reduced to a product of non - nested dotted bubbles with the same orientation .",
    "these dotted bubbles naturally correspond to the basis of @xmath30 given by the complete symmetric functions .",
    "proposition  [ prop_image_thickbub ] identifies natural closed diagrams in the 2-category @xmath12 corresponding to schur polynomials . reducing these closed diagrams using the relations in the 2-category @xmath12 one recovers the jacobi - trudy formula , or giambelli formula , expressing the schur polynomial in terms of complete symmetric functions .    after the categorification @xmath12 was defined in @xcite a related but different approach to categorification appeared in the work of rouquier  @xcite , extending his earlier work with chuang  @xcite .",
    "rouquier defines several 2-categories associated to a symmetrizable kac - moody algebra .",
    "they are related to the 2-categories @xmath25 , however , already in the @xmath16 case these 2-categories appear to be different from @xmath12 . both approaches have their benefits ; for instance , the axiomatics in @xcite ensures that the 2-category @xmath32 has grothendieck ring isomorphic to the integral idempotent form of @xmath33 , while the less stringent axiomatics in @xcite make it easier to check the existence of categorical actions in this sense  @xcite and lead to important results about 2-representations .",
    "we do not know if counterparts of results in the present paper exist for rouquier s 2-categories , since our results crucially depend on all the relations present in the 2-category @xmath12",
    ".    the explicit diagrammatic calculus developed in this article should be useful for enhancing and clarifying constructions of categorical quantum @xmath10 actions .",
    "since the appearance of the more general 2-category @xmath25 , its 2-representation theory ( see ( * ? ? ?",
    "* section 3.4 ) ) , is beginning to be studied .",
    "hill and sussan  @xcite have constructed an action of the 2-category @xmath12 ( over field @xmath34 ) associated to @xmath26 on diagrammatic categories introduced in  @xcite that categorify the irreducible highest weight representation of highest weight @xmath35 .",
    "we expect that various categorical actions of @xmath2 extend to 2-representations of the 2-category @xmath25 , including the categorified representations studied in @xcite .    the formulas derived here for the 2-category @xmath12 might be useful for applications of categorified quantum groups to knot homology .",
    "an action of the 2-category @xmath12 on categories of @xmath36 foams arising in knot homology has been described by mackaay  @xcite .",
    "this action may be related to similar actions , constructed in @xcite , of the diagrammatic soergel category @xcite .",
    "categorified quantum groups appear in geometry in the work of cautis - kamnitzer - licata  @xcite and varagnolo - vasserot  @xcite , see also @xcite .",
    "the diagrammatic calculus developed here should be relevant to the striking new work of webster  @xcite on categorification of reshetikhin - turaev tangle invariants .",

  "abstract_text": [
    "<S> a categorification of the beilinson - lusztig - macpherson form of the quantum sl(2 ) was constructed in the paper arxiv:0803.3652 by the second author . here </S>",
    "<S> we enhance the graphical calculus introduced and developed in that paper to include two - morphisms between divided powers one - morphisms and their compositions . </S>",
    "<S> we obtain explicit diagrammatical formulas for the decomposition of products of divided powers one - morphisms as direct sums of indecomposable one - morphisms ; the latter are in a bijection with the lusztig canonical basis elements . </S>",
    "<S> these formulas have integral coefficients and imply that one of the main results of lauda s paper  identification of the grothendieck ring of his 2-category with the idempotented quantum sl(2)also holds when the 2-category is defined over the ring of integers rather than over a field . </S>"
  ]
}
